# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-30 01:16:23.517136

### Base Program

```py
def smallestFactorization(num: int) -> int:
    if num == 1:
        return 1
    result = 0
    factor = 1
    for i in range(9, 1, -1):
        while num % i == 0:
            num //= i
            result += i * factor
            factor *= 10
            if result > 2**31 - 1:
                return 0
    return result if num == 1 else 0
```

```json
[41]
```

</details>

## Test Case 1

### Modified Program

```py
def smallestFactorization(num: int) -> int:
    if num == 1:
        return 1
    result = 0
    factor = 1
    for i in range(9, 1, -1):
        while num % i == 0:
            num //= i
            result += i * factor
            factor *= 10
            if result > 2 ** 31 - 1:
                return 0
    return result if num == 1 else 0
```

<details>

```
Success
```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py
def smallestFactorization(var_0: int) -> int:
    if var_0 == 1:
        return 1
    result = 0
    factor = 1
    for i in range(9, 1, -1):
        while var_0 % i == 0:
            var_0 //= i
            result += i * factor
            factor *= 10
            if result > 2 ** 31 - 1:
                return 0
    return result if var_0 == 1 else 0
```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py
def smallestFactorization(num: int) -> int:
    if num == 1:
        return 1
    result = 0
    factor = 1
    for i in range(9, 1, -1):
        while num % i == 0:
            num //= i
            result += factor * i
            factor *= 10
            if result > 2 ** 31 + -1:
                return 0
    return result if num == 1 else 0
```

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py
def smallestFactorization(var_1: int) -> int:
    if var_1 == 1:
        return 1
    result = 0
    factor = 1
    for i in range(9, 1, -1):
        while var_1 % i == 0:
            var_1 //= i
            result += factor * i
            factor *= 10
            if result > 2 ** 31 + -1:
                return 0
    return result if var_1 == 1 else 0
```
